 Sam Manekshaw, popularly known as 'sam Bahadur', assumed the position of 8th Chief of the Army Staff of India on 7 June 1969, and was followed by the indo-pak War in December 1971 under his leadership

 On the lines of Israel, the Modi government has decided to guard the border through 'operation Chakravyahu'
 iske tahat hindustan kii seemaa par under water or under ground sensor lagane kii taiyaari ho rahi he
 That is, terrorists will now be able to infiltrate through neither land nor water
 jaankaree ke mutabik, july maheene se hi pakistan se lagi jammu-kashmir or gujarat kisimaamen sensor lagane kaa kaam shuru kar diya jayega
 In the first phase, it is being started as a pilot project at two places in Jammu and Kashmir
 iske tahat paanch-paanch kilometre kii duuri par do jagah sensor lagenge
 BSF will install sensors at an initial cost of 18 to 20 crores for this
 grih mantri karenge ahm baithkgrih mantri shuukravaar shaam 6 baje jammu-kashmir kii seemaa or uski suraksha ko lekar baithak karenge
 There will be talks with all paramilitary forces, state police and BSF officers

 There are many documents of BSF of Aaj Tak, which have information about this scheme
 sarkaar alag-alag companiyon sesurakshake ye upkaran kharid rahi he
 Under this, there are plans to buy under ground sensor, optical fiber cable, radar, electro optic sensor, micro aero stat (balloon)
 seemaa par kaise hogi nigaraneebataya jaataa he ki pakistan se lagi bhartiya seemaa par sabhi electronic system ko ekasaath jodakar uske liye control room banegaa

 kaise kaam karegaa radar or sensorsarhad par laga radar apane chaaron ore yani 360 degree ke ilaake main kisi ghuspaithiye ke aane par sidhe control room ko jaankaree degaa

 yahi nahin, vahiin laga automatic gan aatanki ko palak jhapakate dher kar degaa

 pani ke andar laga sensor vaise hi kaam karegaa jaise jameen ke upar laga sensor kaam karegaa
 Action will be taken as soon as the signal is received in the control room
 kaise kaam karata he electro optical sensordrasal, isamen din or raat main kaam karne vaale camere seemaa par lage rahenge
 They will have direct contact with the control room
 jaise hi seemaa par koi gatividhi dikhi, ye sidhe control room signal denge

 inamen hai quality vaale camere lage honge

 unhone kaha ki vah obamakare (swasthya seva ke kshetra main obama ke kaamon ke liye prayukt) ko tabah karne ke bajaae, isi ko aage badhaane kii niti par amal karenge
 Talking differently is 'talking nonsense'
 ghatana 570 i
 Has been at the peak of the Arab world at its peak
 tab ishwar ne ek sandeshvahak (paigambar) bheja, jisane arab kii jameen ko darindagi se nijaat dilaai or niraakaar ishwar (allaah) kaa parichay dene ke baad manushyon ko ishwar kaa sandesh pahunchaaya, jo allaah kaa 'deen' he
 It was given the name of Islam
 'deen' keval musalamaanon ke liye nahin aayaa, vah sabhi ke liye tha, kyonki buniyadi rup se deen (islam) main achche kaaryon kaa maargdarshan kiya gaya he or bure kaaryon se bachane va rokane ke tareeke bataae gaye hai
 When Mohammed Saheb started spreading Din (islam), almost all Arab tribes accepted the humiliation of Allah by obeying Mohammed
 mohammad ke saath mili kabeelon kii taadaad dekhakar us samay mohammad ke dushman bhi mohammad sahab ke saath aa mili (kuch dikhaave main or kuch dar se)
 But he kept enmity with Mohammed in his heart
 mohammad ke aath june, 632 i
 After his death, these enemies gradually started dominating
 pehle dushmano ne mohammad kii beti fatima jahara ke ghar par hamalaa kiya, jisase ghar kaa darwaja tuutakar fatima jahara par gira or 28 agast, 632 i
 She left this world
 phir kai varsho baad mauka milte hi dushmano ne masjid main namaaj (ishwar kii upasna) padhate samay mohammad ke damaad hazrat ali ke sir par talwaar maar kar unhen shahid kar diya
 The enemies then martyred Mohammad's elder grandson Imam Hasan by poisoning him
 dushman mohammad ke puure parivaar ko khatm karnaa chaahate the, isliye uske baad mohammad ke chote naati imam hossain par dushman dabaav banane lage ki vah us samay ke jabaran bane khalipha 'yajid' (jo naam maatr kaa musalmaan tha) kaa har hukum maane or 'yajid' ko khalipha kabool karen
 Include what Yajid says in Islam and remove what he asks to be removed from Islam
 yani mohammad ke banaae hue deen 'islam' ko badal den
 Imam Hussain was under pressure because he was a favorite grandson of Mohammed
 imam hossain ke bare main mohammad ne kaha tha, 'hossain-o-minni vaa ana minal hossain' yani hossain mujhase hai or main hossain se yani jisane hossain ko dukh diya usne mujhe dukh diya
 The then Khalifa Yazid wanted Hussain to join him, he knew that if Hussain came with him, all Islam would be in his grasp
 lakh dabaav ke baad bhi hossain ne uski kisi bhi baat ko maanane se inkaar kar diya, to yajid ne hossain ko katl karne kii yojana banaai
 Four May, 680 AD
 main imam hossain madeene main apana ghar chhodkar shahar makke pahunche, jahaan unka haj karne kaa iraadaa tha lekin unhen pataa chalaa ki dushman hajiyon ke bhesh main aakar unka katl kar sakate hai
 Hussein did not want to bleed in a holy place like Kaaba, then Hussein changed the intention of Hajj and proceeded towards Kufa
 raste main dushmano kii fouj unhen gher kar karbala le ai
 When the army of the enemy besieged Hussein, at that time the army of the enemy was very thirsty, the Imam provided water to the enemy's army
 yah dekhakar dushman fouj ke sardaar 'hazrat hurr' apane parivaar ke saath hossain se aa mili
 Imam Hussain bought the land on his ground in Karbala, first bought by Hussain, then put his camp in that place
 yajid apane saradaaron ke dwaara lagaataar imam hossain par dabaav banaata gaya ki hossain uski baat maan len, jab imam hossain ne yajid kii sharten nahin maani, to dushmano ne ant main nahar par fouj kaa paharaa laga diya or hossain ke khemon main pani jane par roak laga di gai
